**Stack:** Hand-rolled TypeScript discriminated unions + Zod. No XState, no new frameworks.
**Architecture:** Backend owns state → typed SSE events → dashboard pure consumer. No inference.
**Watch Out For:** Sticky flags (separate RunConfig from RunProgress), strangler fig migration (don't big-bang), substeps as hierarchical states from day one.

Now let me defi...

### Write - 2026-03-10 10:07:42 UTC [11:07:42 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

**SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"

Parallel path — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code removed after validation\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery from persisted state\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState / state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states. Hand-rolled DU is simpler |\n| Shared npm package for types | File-copy sync sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state | Single process, unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue | One workflow at a time |\n| Dynamic step insertion | Step sequence is static |\n\n## Traceability\n\nUpdated during roadmap creation.\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
The file /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md has been updated successfully.

### Write - 2026-03-10 10:07:42 UTC [11:07:42 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

**Result:** ❌ Error
**Output:** ```

retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>celled)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start, separated from RunProgress\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status derived from state machine position — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file written by subscriber — not directly by wave-controller or health API\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits typed SSE event with full WorkflowState snapshot\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived from state machine state (SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands, disabled during transitions\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events directly — no inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code removed after validation\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery from persisted state\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState / state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states. Hand-rolled DU is simpler |\n| Shared npm package for types | File-copy sync sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state | Single process, unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue | One workflow at a time |\n| Dynamic step insertion | Step sequence is static |\n\n## Traceability\n\nUpdated during roadmap creation.\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n"
}
```

Start phase numbering from 15 (v2.1 ended at phase 14)\n2. Derive phases from THIS MILESTONE's requirements only (SM-*, BE-*, SSE-*, UI-*, MIG-*)\n3. Map every requirement to exactly one phase\n4. Derive 2-5 success criteria per phase (observable behaviors)\n5. Validate 100% coverage\n6. Write files immediately (ROADMAP.md, STATE.md, update REQUIREMENTS.md traceability)\n7. Return ROADMAP CREATED with summary\n\nResearch suggests 5-phase structure:\n- Phase 15: Type Definitions (SM-01 through SM-05)\n- Phase 16: Backend State Machine (BE-01 through BE-04)\n- Phase 17: SSE Event Typing (SSE-01 through SSE-03)\n- Phase 18: Dashboard Consumer (UI-01 through UI-05)\n- Phase 19: Migration & Cleanup (MIG-01 through MIG-03)\n\nWrite files first, then return.\n</instructions>\n"

### Write - 2026-03-10 10:07:42 UTC [11:07:42 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>celled)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start, separated from RunProgress\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status derived from state machine position — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file written by subscriber — not directly by wave-controller or health API\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits typed SSE event with full WorkflowState snapshot\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived from state machine state (SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands, disabled during transitions\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events directly — no inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code removed after validation\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery from persisted state\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState / state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states. Hand-rolled DU is simpler |\n| Shared npm package for types | File-copy sync sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state | Single process, unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue | One workflow at a time |\n| Dynamic step insertion | Step sequence is static |\n\n## Traceability\n\nUpdated during roadmap creation.\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n"
}

Derive 2-5 success criteria per phase (observable behaviors)\n5. Validate 100% coverage\n6. Write files immediately (ROADMAP.md, STATE.md, update REQUIREMENTS.md traceability)\n7. Return ROADMAP CREATED with summary\n\nResearch suggests 5-phase structure:\n- Phase 15: Type Definitions (SM-01 through SM-05)\n- Phase 16: Backend State Machine (BE-01 through BE-04)\n- Phase 17: SSE Event Typing (SSE-01 through SSE-03)\n- Phase 18: Dashboard Consumer (UI-01 through UI-05)\n- Phase 19: Migration & Cleanup (MIG-01 through MIG-03)\n\nWrite files first, then return.\n</instructions>\n"

### Write - 2026-03-10 10:07:42 UTC [11:07:42 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

**Result:** ❌ Error
**Output:** ```
<tool_use_error>File has not been read yet. Read it first before writing to it.</tool_use_error>
```

fallback inference\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived from state machine state (SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands, disabled during transitions\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events directly — no inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code removed after validation\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery from persisted state\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState / state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states. Hand-rolled DU is simpler |\n| Shared npm package for types | File-copy sync sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state | Single process, unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue | One workflow at a time |\n| Dynamic step insertion | Step sequence is static |\n\n## Traceability\n\nUpdated during roadmap creation.\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n"
}
```

Start phase numbering from 15 (v2.1 ended at phase 14)\n2. Derive phases from THIS MILESTONE's requirements only (SM-*, BE-*, SSE-*, UI-*, MIG-*)\n3. Map every requirement to exactly one phase\n4. Derive 2-5 success criteria per phase (observable behaviors)\n5. Validate 100% coverage\n6. Write files immediately (ROADMAP.md, STATE.md, update REQUIREMENTS.md traceability)\n7. Return ROADMAP CREATED with summary\n\nResearch suggests 5-phase structure:\n- Phase 15: Type Definitions (SM-01 through SM-05)\n- Phase 16: Backend State Machine (BE-01 through BE-04)\n- Phase 17: SSE Event Typing (SSE-01 through SSE-03)\n- Phase 18: Dashboard Consumer (UI-01 through UI-05)\n- Phase 19: Migration & Cleanup (MIG-01 through MIG-03)\n\nWrite files first, then return.\n</instructions>\n"

### Write - 2026-03-10 10:07:42 UTC [11:07:42 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

**Result:** ❌ Error
**Output:** ```

Derive 2-5 success criteria per phase (observable behaviors)\n5. Validate 100% coverage\n6. Write files immediately (ROADMAP.md, STATE.md, update REQUIREMENTS.md traceability)\n7. ### Write - 2026-03-10 10:07:42 UTC [11:07:42 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

**Result:** ❌ Error
**Output:** ```
<tool_use_error>File has not been read yet. Read it first before writing to it.</tool_use_error>

as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

**Result:** ❌ Error
**Output:** ```
<tool_use_error>File has not been read yet. Read it first before writing to it.</tool_use_error>

v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>celled)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start, separated from RunProgress\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status derived from state machine position — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file written by subscriber — not directly by wave-controller or health API\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits typed SSE event with full WorkflowState snapshot\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived from state machine state (SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands, disabled during transitions\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events directly — no inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code removed after validation\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery from persisted state\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState / state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states. Hand-rolled DU is simpler |\n| Shared npm package for types | File-copy sync sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state | Single process, unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue | One workflow at a time |\n| Dynamic step insertion | Step sequence is static |\n\n## Traceability\n\nUpdated during roadmap creation.\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n"
}

Start phase numbering from 15 (v2.1 ended at phase 14)\n2. Derive phases from THIS MILESTONE's requirements only (SM-*, BE-*, SSE-*, UI-*, MIG-*)\n3. Map every requirement to exactly one phase\n4. Derive 2-5 success criteria per phase (observable behaviors)\n5. Validate 100% coverage\n6. Write files immediately (ROADMAP.md, STATE.md, update REQUIREMENTS.md traceability)\n7. Return ROADMAP CREATED with summary\n\nResearch suggests 5-phase structure:\n- Phase 15: Type Definitions (SM-01 through SM-05)\n- Phase 16: Backend State Machine (BE-01 through BE-04)\n- Phase 17: SSE Event Typing (SSE-01 through SSE-03)\n- Phase 18: Dashboard Consumer (UI-01 through UI-05)\n- Phase 19: Migration & Cleanup (MIG-01 through MIG-03)\n\nWrite files first, then return.\n</instructions>\n"

### Write - 2026-03-10 10:07:42 UTC [11:07:42 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>celled)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start, separated from RunProgress\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status derived from state machine position — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file written by subscriber — not directly by wave-controller or health API\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits typed SSE event with full WorkflowState snapshot\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived from state machine state (SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands, disabled during transitions\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events directly — no inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code removed after validation\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery from persisted state\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState / state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states. Hand-rolled DU is simpler |\n| Shared npm package for types | File-copy sync sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state | Single process, unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue | One workflow at a time |\n| Dynamic step insertion | Step sequence is static |\n\n## Traceability\n\nUpdated during roadmap creation.\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n"
}
```

Derive 2-5 success criteria per phase (observable behaviors)\n5. Validate 100% coverage\n6. Write files immediately (ROADMAP.md, STATE.md, update REQUIREMENTS.md traceability)\n7. Return ROADMAP CREATED with summary\n\nResearch suggests 5-phase structure:\n- Phase 15: Type Definitions (SM-01 through SM-05)\n- Phase 16: Backend State Machine (BE-01 through BE-04)\n- Phase 17: SSE Event Typing (SSE-01 through SSE-03)\n- Phase 18: Dashboard Consumer (UI-01 through UI-05)\n- Phase 19: Migration & Cleanup (MIG-01 through MIG-03)\n\nWrite files first, then return.\n</instructions>\n"

### Write - 2026-03-10 10:07:42 UTC [11:07:42 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md",
  "content": "# Requirements: Coding Project v3.0\n\n**Defined:** 2026-03-10\n**Core Value:** Workflow state management via typed state machine — single source of truth, typed transitions, dashboard as pure consumer\n\n## v3.0 Requirements\n\n### State Machine Core\n\n- [ ] **SM-01**: Workflow state is a TypeScript discriminated union with state-specific data (idle has no data, running has currentStep+substep, paused has pausedAt+mode, completed has summary, failed has error+failedAt, cancelled has no data)\n- [ ] **SM-02**: State transitions are typed — only valid transitions compile (e.g., can't go from idle to paused, can't complete a failed workflow)\n- [ ] **SM-03**: RunConfig (singleStepMode, mockLLM, llmMode, stepIntoSubsteps) is immutable after workflow start and separated from RunProgress — eliminates sticky state bugs\n- [ ] **SM-04**: Step/substep status is derived from state machine position in the step sequence — not stored as separate mutable fields\n- [ ] **SM-05**: Zod schemas validate state at system boundaries (progress file reads, SSE event parsing, API responses)\n\n### Backend Integration\n\n- [ ] **BE-01**: Wave-controller dispatches typed events instead of ad-hoc updateProgress() calls (~50 call sites replaced)\n- [ ] **BE-02**: Health API step-advance endpoint operates on the state machine (dispatch ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO events) instead of mutating JSON flags\n- [ ] **BE-03**: Progress file is written by a subscriber to state transitions — not directly by wave-controller or health API (eliminates race conditions)\n- [ ] **BE-04**: Workflow cancel operates via state machine transition (dispatch CANCEL) — not by mutating progress file fields\n\n### SSE Events\n\n- [ ] **SSE-01**: Every state transition emits a typed SSE event containing the full WorkflowState snapshot — dashboard never needs to infer\n- [ ] **SSE-02**: SSE events use discriminated union types shared between backend and dashboard (file-copy sync, not npm package)\n- [ ] **SSE-03**: SSE reconnection sends full current state on connect — no stale state from missed events\n\n### Dashboard Consumer\n\n- [ ] **UI-01**: Dashboard renders workflow state from typed SSE events only — zero fallback inference, zero position-based guessing\n- [ ] **UI-02**: Substep coloring derived directly from state machine state: pending=light blue, running=dark blue, completed=green (uses SUBSTEP_COLORS from constants)\n- [ ] **UI-03**: Step/Into buttons dispatch typed commands (ADVANCE/ADVANCE_INTO) and are disabled while a transition is in progress\n- [ ] **UI-04**: \"Batch\" label replaced with correct workflow name throughout dashboard\n- [ ] **UI-05**: Redux store receives typed SSE events and stores WorkflowState directly — no intermediate transformation or inference\n\n### Migration\n\n- [ ] **MIG-01**: Parallel path during migration — old updateProgress and new state machine run side-by-side until validated\n- [ ] **MIG-02**: Backward-compatible progress file reader handles both old untyped and new typed format\n- [ ] **MIG-03**: All old inference/fallback code in dashboard removed after state machine is validated\n\n## v3.1 Requirements (Deferred)\n\n- **SM-06**: Crash recovery — hydrate state machine from persisted progress on restart\n- **SM-07**: Workflow history — persist completed workflow states for comparison\n- **UI-06**: State machine inspector panel for debugging transitions in real-time\n- **BE-05**: Retry with feedback as typed state machine loop (retry → running → qa_check → retry/continue)\n\n## Out of Scope\n\n| Feature | Reason |\n|---------|--------|\n| XState or other state machine library | Overkill for ~6 states, ~12 transitions. Hand-rolled DU is simpler and more type-safe |\n| Shared npm package for types | 3 submodules with build+Docker already; file-copy sync is sufficient for ~100 lines |\n| Distributed state / multi-process coordination | Single process, single team — unnecessary complexity |\n| Workflow queue / job scheduler | Pipeline runs one workflow at a time — no queue needed |\n| Dynamic step insertion at runtime | Step sequence is static per workflow definition |\n| GUI state machine editor | Developer tool, not user-facing — code is the editor |\n\n## Traceability\n\n| Requirement | Phase | Status |\n|-------------|-------|--------|\n| SM-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SM-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| BE-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| SSE-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-03 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-04 | TBD | Pending |\n| UI-05 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-01 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-02 | TBD | Pending |\n| MIG-03 | TBD | Pending |\n\n**Coverage:**\n- v3.0 requirements: 20 total\n- Mapped to phases: 0\n- Unmapped: 20\n\n---\n*Requirements defined: 2026-03-10*\n*Last updated: 2026-03-10 after initial definition*\n"
}
```

**Result:** ❌ Error
**Output:** ```
<tool_use_error>File has not been read yet. Read it first before writing to it.</tool_use_error>
```
